I try tea shops' black milk tea as a gauge of their drink quality and was impressed by Raretea's. The boba pearls were close to perfect; the ideal consistency and slightly sweet. The black milk tea also was very good. The interior/atmosphere was not as friendly to hanging out (limited seating and small space), but as a grab-and-go, it did the trick.</review>

< Review>
Jeff with Triton far exceeded our expectations for transforming our pool to where it needed to be.

As new home owners, we acquired a 25k gallon pool that either needed a complete water change or a Reverse Osmosis water renew (CYA Acid Levels too high - Chlorine Lock) AND the pool pump filter was broken and in need of repair. We care for our environment and were looking for a way to reuse the water that we have in the pool.

While we were dealing with the filter pump for over a month, Jeff was extremely patient and friendly through the whole process. Jeff checked in regularly on the status of the filter and rescheduled a few times while we waited for the repairs. Jeff also gave us guidance on how to best resolve the algae issue before providing the water renew service also providing a before and after water report when he  was done.

As you can see the results are night and day! We will definitely use Jeff again in a few years when it is time to renew the water again. Our family of 4 is now enjoying our pool regularly thanks to Triton!<//Review>

Park is pretty but very difficult access to the river.  Dangerous really.  Took my dog there after googling dog parks.  No fence for dogs but nice walking paths except for the people that were inhabiting the park.  One guy stumbled out of the bathroom with his pants zipper down and his parts out.  Ok that could happen to anyone forgetting but my very sweet dog was as disturbed as I was.   Relieved to see a couple walking in the park.  But bicycle riders were riding up to the table the couple decided to sit.  Some presents he was handing out to the grown men riding kids bikes?
Nice views of the river through wooded trees and a blanket of leaves covered a wooded area which had the smell of fall.  Then a path in high grass that seem to lead to Drake Road seemed interesting and my dog wanted to check it out.   Seemed a couple of guys made up a pretty good set up with grill, tents, beds...I figured one was the one that hangs out in town because of the wheel chair.  I was politely given a courteous hello.  Gave it one star because of dangerous access to the river and no place for dog to go off leash.<//text>

< review>
I came to Chinatown late around 7:00pm local time. I am supposed most stores are closed. Some restaurants are open with no customers already. Another restaurant are lined up with many people. I really don't don't want a big dinner as I travel alone for business. So I decided to come in New Lun Ting Cafe. I ordered a beef chow fun. It came with a free soup, it tastes really good. Before she also give me a free fried dumpling before serving. Chow fun tasted very good too.</review>

<time>1576471731945<//time><gmapID>0x808580f4bcdea927:0x25056e246e8c0d68<//gmapID><username>Hvey Jci Cheong</username>< user>
100146984739362588950< /user>
<review>Not even joking when I say this place has provided the cheapest decent meal I've eaten since landing in America. They had a 3-dish and a soup meal set for 23 dollars. But we ordered more. Very original Chinese cuisine. Ordered some pork and cabbage dumpling/Woh tip, Mongolian fried fish, beef brisket with foochuk/beancurd sheet (this is the bomb. The beef came apart just as you chew it. Nicely stewed), prawns with scrambled eggs. There is also stir fried beef with kailan. The business is about 100 years old but the current owners (two sisters and their folks) have been running the place for the last 50 years. They're also famous for their pork chops but we haven't got the stomach space for it. perhaps, next time. The sisters who ran the place were exceptionally gracious and made it all the more homely. I would definitely recommend this to whoever who is planning a day tour to Chinatown in San Francisco</review></record></dataset><record>

Blue-collar Chinese diner, with the usual mix of carbolicious noodle and rice dishes.

I'm a fan of the grilled tilapia, which comes with either a side of corn or cabbage. A little lemon and mayo atop and it's a relatively healthy meal.

Not a big hit on your wallet either since everything is around $7-8.

Can be swamped during lunch hours, and the waitress tends to discourage you from ordering anything they can't just scoop over rice for you, but persist!<//text>

< Review>
It's a simple park with enough to keep you entertained for a bit. There is a two story play area for kids that include jungle gyms, Bridges and slides. The floor is made of rubber so that children don't get hurt too badly if they fall. Can't forget the swings and mini water park. They have one basketball court and two baseball fields (for youth teams use only). They have a few picnic tables and a tables to use for small family events.  Lastly, the park has a cement path that circles the park, which is around 400 meters, so it's actually a pretty cool spot to go for a jog.< /Review>
